# 1. Search and get new forecast location id
Base url: https://api.foreca.net/locations/search/searchrequest.json?limit=limit&lang=lang

#### Request params
| URL Parameter      | Description                                              |
| ------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------- |
| searchrequest.json | Instead of "searchrequest", paste here your search query |
| limit              | Limit of result items (locations) in response            |
| lang               | Language of response json                                |

#### Response parsing
| JSON key                                        | Value description                              |
| ----------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------- |
| query                                           | Your search query                              |
| language                                        | Response language                              |
| results                                         | Json array of found locations                  |
| id                                              | Id of location for requesting weather forecast |
| lon                                             | Longitude of location                          |
| lat                                             | Latitude of location                           |
| type                                            | **?UNKNOWN?**                                  |
| adm1_id-adm3_id                                 | **?UNKNOWN?**                                  |
| population                                      | People count of location                       |
| countryId                                       | ID of country (short country name)             |
| timezone                                        | Time zone of locations                         |
| preference                                      | **?UNKNOWN?**                                  |
| warningSources                                  | Source country of weather warnings??           |
| name                                            | Geographical name of location                  |
| countryName                                     | Short country name                             |
| countryId                                       | ID of country (short country name)             |
| defaultName, defaultCountryName, defaultAdmName | Default names??                                |


### Sample request
Request URL: https://api.foreca.net/locations/search/new%20york.json?limit=5&lang=en

Response:

# 2. All forecast (15mins, hourly, daily, etc.)
Base url: https://api.foreca.net/mobile/id_of_location.json?lang=lang

#### Request params
| URL Parameter       | Description                                                                        |
| ------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| id_of_location.json | ID of location, received from [search](#1-search-and-get-new-forecast-location-id) |
| lang                | Language of response json                                                          |

#### Response parsing
#### **Main keys**
| JSON key   | Value description                            |
| ---------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| time       | Time of last forecast update                 |
| temp       | Temperature in Celsius                       |
| temp_raw   | Temperature in Celsius without rounding      |
| flike      | Feels-like temperature in in Celsius         |
| flike_fin  | **??UNKNOWN??**                              |
| temp_f     | Temperature in Fahrenheit                    |
| prec       | Precipitation amount in milimiters           |
| prl        | **??UNKNOWN??**                              |
| prs        | **Precipitation too??**                      |
| windd      | Wind direction angle                         |
| winds      | Wind speed in m/s                            |
| winds_max  | Maximum wind speed in m/s                    |
| rhum       | Humidity in percent                          |
| symb       | Weather [symbol](#Weather-simbol)            |
| dewp       | **??UNKNOWN??**                              |
| pres       | Pressure in hPa but **NOT VERY ACCURATE**    |
| pres_stn   | More accurate pressure in hPa                |
| uwi        | **??UNKNOWN??**                              |
| uwi_raw    | **??UNKNOWN??**                              |
| moon       | **Fullness of the moon maybe in percents??** |
| cloudiness | **Cloudiness maybe in percents??**           |
| daylen     | Length of the day in minutes                 |
| sunrise    | Time of the sunrise                          |
| sunset     | Time of the sunset                           |
| daylen_h   | Hour lenght of the day                       |
| daylen_m   | Minute lenght of the day                     |


#### **Sections**
| JSON section | Description                                      |
| ------------ | ------------------------------------------------ |
| obs          | **Weather forecast from nearby meteostations??** |
| nowcast      | Current weather forecast                         |
| 15m          | Weather forecast for next 15 minutes             |
| hourly       | Hourly weather forecast for 10 days              |
| daily        | Daily weather forecast for 10 days               |
| maps         | Weather map, but don't know how to use it        |
| ranges       | **Calibration info maybe??**                     |
| biomet       | **Biometric forecast??(like UV-index, etc.)**    |

### Sample request
Request URL: https://api.foreca.net/mobile/105128581.json?lang=en

# 3. Weather forecast symbol
Base url: https://www.foreca.com/public/images/symbols/id_of_symbol.svg

#### Request params
| URL Parameter    | Description                                   |
| ---------------- | --------------------------------------------- |
| id_of_symbol.svg | [Symbol](#main-keys) id from weather forecast |

### Sample request
Request URL: https://www.foreca.com/public/images/symbols/d400.svg

Response: 

![d400 symbol](https://www.foreca.com/public/images/symbols/d400.svg)

# 3. Wind symbol
Base url: https://www.foreca.com/public/images/wind/blue/id_of_symbol.svg

#### Request params
| URL Parameter    | Description                                |
| ---------------- | ------------------------------------------ |
| id_of_symbol.svg | [Symbol](#main-keys) id from wind forecast |

### Sample request
Request URL: https://www.foreca.com/public/images/wind/blue/w315.svg

Response: 

<img src="https://www.foreca.com/public/images/wind/blue/w315.svg" alt="d400 symbol" width="50"/>
